# Codex BRIEF review — I-gen-004 / GH #496: capture + store the V4 Pro reasoning trace separately

HARD ITERATION CAP: 5 per document. This is iter 3 of 5.
- Front-load ALL real findings in iter 1. No drip-feeding across iterations.
- Same quality bar regardless of iteration count.
- "Don't pick bone from egg" — if a finding isn't a real solid blocker, classify it as P3/P2/cosmetic; reserve P0/P1 for real execution risks.
- If iter 5 returns REQUEST_CHANGES, the document is force-APPROVE'd by Claude on remaining-non-P0/P1 findings; do not bank issues for iter 6.
- If you detect "I'm holding back a P1 to surface in the next round" — DON'T. Surface it now. The 5-cap means iter 6 doesn't exist; banked findings die at iter 5.
- Verdict APPROVE iff zero NOVEL P0 AND zero continuing P0 AND zero P1.

## 0. What you are reviewing

A **BRIEF review** (iter 3) — verify the acceptance criteria + approach are
correct and complete BEFORE the diff is written.

## 0.1 Iter-1 + iter-2 findings — addressed

- **P1-001** (reasoning→content promotion) → `content_source` field + §2.3.
- **P1-002** (scope = all generator LLM calls) → §2.2.
- **P1-003** (signed bundle path) → §2.5.
- **P1-004** (capture point too high — misses internal `generate_retry`
  and the `ReasoningFirstTruncationError` raise path) → **§2.6: capture is
  moved to the `OpenRouterClient` level, before any retry / promotion /
  extraction / raise.**
- **P2-001** (Pipeline-A manifest write sites) → §2.5: trace injection
  centralized in `augment_v6_manifest()`.
- **P2-002** (`live_deepseek_generator.generate_live_draft()`) → §2.2 scope
  note.
- **P2-003** (bundle sidecar-data interface) → §2.5 spells out the
  `build_manifest_and_files()` interface change.

## 1. The issue (GH #496 / I-gen-004)

Operator directive 2026-05-14: "keep the **whole** reasoning log and output
content separated and properly stored, transparently." DeepSeek V4 Pro is
reasoning-first (one outline call: `content=1791 B` + `reasoning=17521 B`).
POLARIS currently discards `response.reasoning`. Dependency I-gen-003 (#495)
is complete.

## 2. Proposed approach

### 2.1 Run-scoped reasoning-trace collector

A run-scoped collector created at run start. It accumulates one record per
raw completed provider response and flushes `reasoning_trace.jsonl` at run
end.

### 2.2 Capture scope — every generator-side LLM call

`_call_section` (+ regen), `_call_outline` (+ retry), sentence-repair
(I-bug-108), `_call_limitations`, `_call_trial_summary_table` (+ fallback),
`_call_m50_per_trial_subsection`, analyst synthesis, fact-dedup rewrite,
cross-trial / cross-jurisdiction / regulatory synthesizers, and the V30
contract-slot / regulatory `_m63_llm_call` path. `live_deepseek_generator.
generate_live_draft()` is covered **when invoked inside a run that carries
a collector**; its standalone-legacy-script invocation (no run context) is
explicitly out of scope (a record cannot be routed without a run).

### 2.3 The reasoning→content promotion (P1-001)

`openrouter_client.py` promotes reasoning→content for reasoning-first models
when `content` is empty (I-bug-088 recovery). The trace record carries
`content_source ∈ {direct, promoted_from_reasoning}`; `reasoning_text`
always records the raw model reasoning channel; `content_text` records what
was used as section content. When `promoted_from_reasoning`, the two
legitimately overlap — the trace discloses it.

### 2.4 Record schema (one JSON object per raw completed provider response)

`{call_id, parent_call_id, section, call_type, regen_reason, attempt_n,
model, status, reasoning_text, content_text, content_source, input_tokens,
output_tokens, reasoning_tokens, timestamp}`

- `call_type ∈ {outline, section, repair, regen, limitations, trial_table,
  m50_subsection, analyst_synthesis, fact_dedup, contract_slot, regulatory}`.
- `status ∈ {ok, retry, truncated, error}` — distinguishes a clean
  response from an internal-retry attempt, a `ReasoningFirstTruncationError`
  capture, and a hard error.
- `regen_reason` disambiguates `regen` (strict-verify retry / M44 / M47);
  `parent_call_id` links a regen/repair/retry to its parent.

### 2.5 Capture point — at the `OpenRouterClient` level (P1-004)

The capture must sit **below** the generator call sites, because
`OpenRouterClient.generate()` internally retries (`generate_retry`),
promotes reasoning→content, extracts `</think>`, and **raises
`ReasoningFirstTruncationError`** — the last of which is exactly the
reasoning-first case #496 exists to preserve, and a generator-call-site
wrapper would never see it.

- The `OpenRouterClient` gains an optional run-scoped `reasoning_sink`
  (a collector handle / callback, default `None` = no-op — keeps the
  client usable outside the generator).
- At the point in `_call` / `generate` where a **raw completed provider
  response** first exists, the client appends a record to the sink —
  BEFORE any promotion, `</think>` extraction, retry decision, or raise.
- The internal `generate_retry` path appends one record per attempt
  (`status=retry` for superseded attempts).
- The `ReasoningFirstTruncationError` path appends the raw truncated
  response (`status=truncated`) to the sink **before raising** — so the
  reasoning is preserved even though the call "fails" and `_call_section`
  catches the exception and returns an empty draft.
- Generator-call context (`section`, `call_type`, `attempt_n`) is supplied
  by the caller via a per-call context the client threads onto the record.

### 2.6 Store + manifest + signed bundle (P1-003, P2-001, P2-003)

- Per run: `reasoning_trace.jsonl` in the run output dir.
- Manifest: trace-file injection is centralized in
  `audit_ir/manifest_augment.py::augment_v6_manifest()` so all three
  `scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py` manifest paths (success / abort / error)
  reference it uniformly — not bolted onto each write site.
- Signed bundle: `build_slice_chain()` returns `(decision, pool, report)`
  and `build_manifest_and_files()` currently takes no sidecar input.
  `build_manifest_and_files()` gains an explicit optional
  `extra_files`/artifact-dir parameter; the `/runs/{run_id}/bundle.tar.gz`
  bridge passes `reasoning_trace.jsonl` through it; a new
  `content_type=reasoning_trace` is added so the file is included AND
  hashed in the signed manifest. A bundle test asserts the trace file is
  present and hashed under that content type.
- `REVIEWER_README.md` (+ `/transparency` or the bundle README) documents
  the trace as **model-process evidence, NOT verified claims**.

## 3. Acceptance criteria (verify correct + complete)

1. A run-scoped collector captures `reasoning` + `reasoning_tokens` from
   **every raw completed provider response** for generator-side LLM calls
   (§2.2), via an `OpenRouterClient`-level sink (§2.5) — including internal
   `generate_retry` attempts and the `ReasoningFirstTruncationError` path.
2. Per-run `reasoning_trace.jsonl`, one record per response with the §2.4
   schema; reasoning text lives in the jsonl only — never independently
   merged into `report.md` / `verified_text` / the verified-sentence stream.
3. `manifest.json` references the trace (via `augment_v6_manifest()`); the
   signed `bundle.tar.gz` includes + hashes it under
   `content_type=reasoning_trace`.
4. `/transparency` or bundle `REVIEWER_README.md` documents the trace as
   process evidence, not claims.
5. **Separation invariant + tests:** `reasoning_trace.jsonl` is a separate
   artifact; `strict_verify` runs on the content channel only, never
   independently on `reasoning_text`. Tests: (a) a V4-Pro-style
   `content='', reasoning='SENTINEL'` response → captured, recorded
   `content_source=promoted_from_reasoning`; (b) the internal
   `generate_retry` path → each attempt recorded; (c) the
   `ReasoningFirstTruncationError` path → the truncated raw response
   recorded `status=truncated` before the raise; (d) a normal call →
   `reasoning_text` (the CoT) never appears in `report.md`.
6. Non-reasoning models (`reasoning` empty/None) → record still written,
   empty `reasoning_text`, uniform schema, no crash.
7. Codex diff review APPROVE.

**Diff-size note:** client-level capture + every generator call + manifest
+ signed-bundle interface + tests will likely exceed the 200-LOC isolated-
CODE cap; this is inherent to the operator's "whole reasoning log" scope —
request the Codex diff-review exemption rather than narrowing coverage.

 1093:         messages: list[dict[str, str]],
 1094:         call_type: str,
 1095:         reasoning_enabled: bool = True,
 1096:         reasoning_effort: str = "high",
 1097:         temperature: float = 0.7,
 1098:         max_tokens: int = 16384,
 1099:         response_format: Optional[dict] = None,
 1100:         timeout: Optional[float] = None,
 1101:         reasoning_max_tokens: Optional[int] = None,
 1102:         reasoning_exclude: Optional[bool] = None,
 1103:     ) -> LLMResponse:
 1104:         """Make a single API call to OpenRouter.
 1105: 
 1106:         A8.2: Acquires global concurrency semaphore before executing.
 1107:         This prevents GPU OOM on sovereign deployments and 429 rate
 1108:         limits on cloud APIs by limiting parallel LLM calls.
 1109:         """
 1110:         # A8.2: Global concurrency control
 1111:         from src.providers.llm_provider import get_semaphore
 1112:         semaphore = get_semaphore()
 1113:         async with semaphore:
 1114:             return await self._call_impl(
 1115:                 messages, call_type, reasoning_enabled, reasoning_effort,
 1116:                 temperature, max_tokens, response_format, timeout,
 1117:                 reasoning_max_tokens, reasoning_exclude,
 1118:             )
 1119: 
 1120:     async def _call_impl(
 1121:         self,
 1122:         messages: list[dict[str, str]],
 1123:         call_type: str,
 1124:         reasoning_enabled: bool = True,
 1125:         reasoning_effort: str = "high",
 1126:         temperature: float = 0.7,
 1127:         max_tokens: int = 16384,
 1128:         response_format: Optional[dict] = None,
 1129:         timeout: Optional[float] = None,
 1130:         reasoning_max_tokens: Optional[int] = None,
 1131:         reasoning_exclude: Optional[bool] = None,
 1132:     ) -> LLMResponse:
 1133:         """Internal implementation — called within semaphore context."""
 1134:         # FIX-402: Short-circuit all calls once 402 Payment Required is received.
 1135:         if OpenRouterClient._billing_exhausted:
 1136:             raise BillingExhaustedException(
 1137:                 "OpenRouter billing exhausted (402 circuit breaker OPEN). "
 1138:                 "No API calls will be attempted."
 1139:             )
 1140: 
 1141:         if self.usage.budget_exhausted:
 1142:             raise BudgetExhaustedError(
 1143:                 f"Budget exhausted: ${self.usage.total_cost_usd:.2f} "
 1144:                 f">= ${self.usage.budget_usd:.2f}"
 1145:             )
 1146: 
 1147:         # R-2: check the shared per-run budget cap. Each client
 1148:         # contributes to _RUN_COST_USD after each call; here we abort
 1149:         # early if the cap is already breached rather than fire another
 1150:         # call and discover the overage after the fact.
 1151:         check_run_budget(anticipated_additional=0.0)
 1152: 
 1153:         # K2-3: Filter reasoning_content: null from messages to prevent
 1154:         # prompt pollution (literal "null" causes model confusion).
 1155:         sanitized_messages = []
 1156:         for msg in messages:
 1157:             clean_msg = {k: v for k, v in msg.items() if v is not None}
 1158:             sanitized_messages.append(clean_msg)
 1159: 
 1160:         body: dict[str, Any] = {
 1161:             "model": self.model,
 1162:             "messages": sanitized_messages,
 1163:             "temperature": temperature,
 1164:             "max_tokens": max_tokens,
 1165:             "stream": True,
 1166:         }
 1167: 
 1168:         # GLM-5 TWO-POOL ARCHITECTURE:
 1169:         # Pool 1 (reasoning field): reasoning tokens → logged for monitoring
 1170:         # Pool 2 (content field): actual output → used for report
 1171:         # GLM-5 returns BOTH when max_tokens is sufficient (tested:
 1172:         #   max_tokens=2000 → 1313 chars content + 5868 chars reasoning).
 1173:         # CRITICAL: Never merge reasoning into content. Never disable reasoning.
 1174:         # Reasoning drives analytical quality (SO WHAT, contradictions, GRADE).
 1175:         if self.model in _ALWAYS_REASON_MODELS:
 1176:             # W1.2 merge-not-replace: defaults fill only keys the caller didn't set.
 1177:             # Caller-passed reasoning_max_tokens / reasoning_exclude now reach the API.
 1178:             reasoning_dict: dict[str, Any] = {"exclude": False}
 1179:             if reasoning_exclude is not None:
 1180:                 reasoning_dict["exclude"] = reasoning_exclude
 1181:             if reasoning_max_tokens is not None:
 1182:                 # OpenRouter constraint: effort and max_tokens are mutually exclusive.
 1183:                 reasoning_dict["max_tokens"] = reasoning_max_tokens
 1184:             else:
 1185:                 reasoning_dict["effort"] = reasoning_effort or "high"
 1186:             body["reasoning"] = reasoning_dict
 1187:             body["temperature"] = 1.0  # GLM-5 docs: temp 1.0 for thinking
 1188:             # Enforce minimum max_tokens so reasoning doesn't starve content.
 1189:             # At max_tokens<2000, GLM-5 spends entire budget on reasoning,
 1190:             # leaving content empty. Tested: 2000 → 1313 chars content.
 1191:             _min_tokens = int(os.getenv("PG_GLM5_MIN_MAX_TOKENS", "4096"))
 1192:             if body.get("max_tokens", 0) < _min_tokens:
 1193:                 body["max_tokens"] = _min_tokens
 1194:         elif reasoning_enabled:
 1195:             reasoning_dict = {"effort": reasoning_effort, "enabled": True}
 1196:             if reasoning_max_tokens is not None:
 1197:                 reasoning_dict.pop("effort", None)
 1198:                 reasoning_dict["max_tokens"] = reasoning_max_tokens
 1199:             if reasoning_exclude is not None:
 1200:                 reasoning_dict["exclude"] = reasoning_exclude
 1201:             body["reasoning"] = reasoning_dict
 1202:         elif self.model in _REASONING_FIRST_MODELS:
 1203:             # I-bug-089: caller wants reasoning_enabled=False but this model
 1204:             # (e.g. DeepSeek V4 Pro/Flash) routes to reasoning_content anyway.
 1205:             # Cap reasoning at 40% of max_tokens so 60% is reserved for content,
 1206:             # preventing token-starvation where the planning eats the budget
 1207:             # and the model never gets to write the answer. Caller-passed
 1208:             # reasoning_max_tokens / reasoning_exclude still take precedence.
 1209:             reasoning_dict = {"exclude": False}
 1210:             if reasoning_exclude is not None:
 1211:                 reasoning_dict["exclude"] = reasoning_exclude
 1212:             if reasoning_max_tokens is not None:
 1213:                 reasoning_dict["max_tokens"] = reasoning_max_tokens
 1214:             else:
 1215:                 reasoning_dict["max_tokens"] = max(int(max_tokens * 0.4), 100)
 1216:             body["reasoning"] = reasoning_dict
 1217:             # I-bug-090 / I-gen-003: OpenRouter does NOT enforce
 1218:             # reasoning.max_tokens for V4 Pro on the provider side — the
 1219:             # model reasons until it hits the OVERALL max_tokens ceiling.
 1220:             # The I-bug-090 estimate of "~2500 reasoning tokens" was wrong:
 1221:             # the I-gen-003 V4 Pro smoke (2026-05-14) showed V4 Pro emit
 1222:             # 21284 chars (~5300+ tokens) of reasoning and STILL truncate
 1223:             # mid-sentence at the 6000-token ceiling — it never reached the
 1224:             # content. Floor must give V4 Pro room to FINISH planning AND
 1225:             # write the cited paragraph. 20000 floor → ~5-8k reasoning +
 1226:             # ~12-15k content headroom. Env-tunable. Smoke #3 (2026-05-14)
 1227:             # confirmed: at 20000, V4 Pro completed all 6 sections with
 1228:             # zero ReasoningFirstTruncationError.
 1229:             _min_tokens = int(os.getenv("PG_REASONING_FIRST_MIN_MAX_TOKENS", "20000"))
 1230:             if body.get("max_tokens", 0) < _min_tokens:
 1231:                 body["max_tokens"] = _min_tokens
 1232: 
 1233:         if response_format:
 1234:             body["response_format"] = response_format
 1235:             # FIX-QWEN-2: Use non-streaming for json_object responses.
 1236:             # Alibaba provider (Qwen 3.5 Plus) returns 502 on json_object+stream.

 1874:     async def generate(
 1875:         self,
 1876:         prompt: str,
 1877:         system: str = "",
 1878:         max_tokens: int = 4096,
 1879:         temperature: float = 0.7,
 1880:         timeout: Optional[float] = None,
 1881:         reasoning_max_tokens: Optional[int] = None,
 1882:         reasoning_exclude: Optional[bool] = None,
 1883:     ) -> LLMResponse:
 1884:         """
 1885:         Prose/output call — reasoning OFF, clean output only.
 1886: 
 1887:         Use for: section writing, report prose, summaries.
 1888: 
 1889:         No CoT in the output. No reasoning field. Just clean text.
 1890: 
 1891:         COT-2: If content is empty but reasoning has substance, try to
 1892:         extract the answer from reasoning (provider misroute). If that
 1893:         fails, retry once (OpenRouter may re-route to a different provider).
 1894:         """
 1895:         messages = []
 1896:         if system:
 1897:             messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system})
 1898:         messages.append({"role": "user", "content": prompt})
 1899: 
 1900:         result = await self._call(
 1901:             messages=messages,
 1902:             call_type="generate",
 1903:             reasoning_enabled=False,
 1904:             temperature=temperature,
 1905:             max_tokens=max_tokens,
 1906:             timeout=timeout or DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
 1907:             reasoning_max_tokens=reasoning_max_tokens,
 1908:             reasoning_exclude=reasoning_exclude,
 1909:         )
 1910: 
 1911:         # TWO-POOL: Content field = output. Reasoning field = logged separately.
 1912:         # For GLM-5, both pools are populated when max_tokens is sufficient.
 1913:         # Log reasoning for monitoring but NEVER merge into content.
 1914:         if result.reasoning and self.model in _ALWAYS_REASON_MODELS:
 1915:             logger.info(
 1916:                 "[polaris graph] POOL-1: Reasoning logged (%d chars) for generate()",
 1917:                 len(result.reasoning),
 1918:             )
 1919: 
 1920:         if result.content and result.content.strip():
 1921:             return result
 1922: 
 1923:         # Fallback: content empty (max_tokens too low or provider issue).
 1924:         # Try </think> extraction from reasoning as last resort.
 1925:         if result.reasoning:
 1926:             extracted = _extract_answer_from_reasoning(result.reasoning)
 1927:             if extracted:
 1928:                 logger.warning(
 1929:                     "[polaris graph] POOL-FALLBACK: generate() content empty — "
 1930:                     "recovered %d chars from reasoning via </think> split",
 1931:                     len(extracted),
 1932:                 )
 1933:                 result = LLMResponse(
 1934:                     content=extracted,
 1935:                     reasoning=result.reasoning,
 1936:                     input_tokens=result.input_tokens,
 1937:                     output_tokens=result.output_tokens,
 1938:                     reasoning_tokens=result.reasoning_tokens,
 1939:                     model=result.model,
 1940:                     duration_ms=result.duration_ms,
 1941:                     raw_response=result.raw_response,
 1942:                 )
 1943:             elif self.model in _ALWAYS_REASON_MODELS:
 1944:                 # FIX-GLM5: Models that always reason don't use </think> tags.
 1945:                 # Use reasoning directly as content (same as COT-3 free-form).
 1946:                 # FIX-GLM5-COT: Strip chain-of-thought markers from reasoning
 1947:                 # before using as content. GLM-5 puts "1. **Analyze the Request:**"
 1948:                 # and "The user wants..." thinking before the actual output.
 1949:                 _cleaned_reasoning = result.reasoning
 1950:                 import re as _re
 1951: 
 1952:                 # Strategy 1: Find end of numbered thinking steps pattern
 1953:                 # GLM-5 uses "1. **Analyze...**\n2. **Draft...**\n" then output
 1954:                 _thinking_block = _re.search(
 1955:                     r"\n(?=(?:##\s|[A-Z][a-z]{3,}.*(?:\[|\(95%|MD\s|SMD\s|HR\s|RR\s|OR\s)))",
 1956:                     _cleaned_reasoning,
 1957:                 )
 1958: 
 1959:                 # Strategy 2: Find after "Now let me" / "Here is" / "Output:" patterns
 1960:                 if not _thinking_block or _thinking_block.start() < 50:
 1961:                     _thinking_block = _re.search(
 1962:                         r"\n(?:(?:Now let me|Here is|Here's|Output:?|The revised|The edited|REVISED|EDITED).*\n)",
 1963:                         _cleaned_reasoning,
 1964:                         _re.IGNORECASE,
 1965:                     )
 1966:                     if _thinking_block:
 1967:                         # Use the end of the "Now let me" line as the start of real content
 1968:                         _tb_pos = _thinking_block.end()
 1969:                         class _PosHolder:
 1970:                             def start(self):
 1971:                                 return _tb_pos
 1972:                         _thinking_block = _PosHolder()
 1973: 
 1974:                 # Strategy 3: Original domain-keyword detection
 1975:                 if not _thinking_block or _thinking_block.start() < 50:
 1976:                     _thinking_block = _re.search(
 1977:                         r"(?:^|\n)(?=[A-Z][a-z].*(?:\[CITE:|\[\d+\]|fasting|study|meta|trial|evidence|research|protocol|clinical))",
 1978:                         _cleaned_reasoning,
 1979:                     )
 1980: 
 1981:                 if _thinking_block and _thinking_block.start() > 100:
 1982:                     _cleaned_reasoning = _cleaned_reasoning[_thinking_block.start():].lstrip()
 1983:                     logger.info(
 1984:                         "[polaris graph] FIX-GLM5-COT: Stripped %d chars CoT prefix "
 1985:                         "from generate() reasoning",
 1986:                         _thinking_block.start(),
 1987:                     )
 1988:                 logger.info(
 1989:                     "[polaris graph] FIX-GLM5: generate() using reasoning as "
 1990:                     "content for always-reason model %s (%d chars)",
 1991:                     self.model, len(_cleaned_reasoning),
 1992:                 )
 1993:                 result = LLMResponse(
 1994:                     content=_cleaned_reasoning,
 1995:                     reasoning=result.reasoning,
 1996:                     input_tokens=result.input_tokens,
 1997:                     output_tokens=result.output_tokens,
 1998:                     reasoning_tokens=result.reasoning_tokens,
 1999:                     model=result.model,
 2000:                     duration_ms=result.duration_ms,
 2001:                     raw_response=result.raw_response,
 2002:                 )
 2003:             elif len(result.reasoning.strip()) >= 100:
 2004:                 # I-bug-088: response-shape-centric normalization for
 2005:                 # reasoning-first models (e.g. DeepSeek V4 Pro) that route
 2006:                 # ALL assistant tokens to reasoning_content, leave content
 2007:                 # empty, and emit no </think> tag. The prior COT-2 retry
 2008:                 # cannot recover this — the provider produces the same shape
 2009:                 # on retry. Use raw reasoning as the answer; raw is preserved
 2010:                 # in result.reasoning for tracing. Threshold of 100 chars
 2011:                 # guards against treating a near-empty reasoning blip as a
 2012:                 # full answer.
 2013:                 #
 2014:                 # I-bug-089: detect token-starvation case where the model
 2015:                 # ran out of budget mid-planning. If reasoning has no
 2016:                 # provenance markers AND ends mid-sentence, the model
 2017:                 # never wrote the answer — fail loud so caller can retry
 2018:                 # with bigger budget instead of promoting planning prelude.
 2019:                 _reasoning_clean = result.reasoning.rstrip()
 2020:                 if (
 2021:                     "[#ev:" not in result.reasoning
 2022:                     and not _reasoning_clean.endswith((".", "!", "?", '"'))
 2023:                 ):
 2024:                     self.usage.total_errors += 1
 2025:                     raise ReasoningFirstTruncationError(
 2026:                         f"I-bug-089: reasoning-first model {self.model} "

 2028:                         f"has {len(result.reasoning)} chars but no [#ev:] "

 2030:                         f"budget. SF-15 fail-loud."
 2031:                     )
 2032:                 logger.warning(
 2033:                     "[polaris graph] I-bug-088: generate() content empty, "
 2034:                     "reasoning has %d chars and no </think> tag. Model %s is "
 2035:                     "reasoning-first — using reasoning as content directly.",
 2036:                     len(result.reasoning), self.model,
 2037:                 )
 2038:                 result = LLMResponse(
 2039:                     content=result.reasoning,
 2040:                     reasoning=result.reasoning,
 2041:                     input_tokens=result.input_tokens,
 2042:                     output_tokens=result.output_tokens,
 2043:                     reasoning_tokens=result.reasoning_tokens,
 2044:                     model=result.model,
 2045:                     duration_ms=result.duration_ms,
 2046:                     raw_response=result.raw_response,
 2047:                 )
 2048:             else:
 2049:                 # Reasoning is too sparse to be a real answer — retry once
 2050:                 # (provider may re-route on retry).
 2051:                 logger.warning(
 2052:                     "[polaris graph] COT-2: generate() content empty, "
 2053:                     "reasoning sparse (%d chars). Retrying once.",
 2054:                     len(result.reasoning),
 2055:                 )
 2056:                 result = await self._call(
 2057:                     messages=messages,
 2058:                     call_type="generate_retry",
 2059:                     reasoning_enabled=False,
 2060:                     temperature=temperature,
 2061:                     max_tokens=max_tokens,
 2062:                     timeout=timeout or DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
 2063:                 )
 2064:                 # Try extraction on retry result too
 2065:                 if not result.content.strip() and result.reasoning:
 2066:                     extracted = _extract_answer_from_reasoning(result.reasoning)
 2067:                     if extracted:
 2068:                         result = LLMResponse(

 2071:                             input_tokens=result.input_tokens,

 2073:                             reasoning_tokens=result.reasoning_tokens,
 2074:                             model=result.model,
 2075:                             duration_ms=result.duration_ms,
 2076:                             raw_response=result.raw_response,
 2077:                         )

  470:     # Build a compact evidence summary (title + tier + 160 chars of

 1866:     """Generate a "Trial Summary" markdown table from verified prose.

 1868:     Returns (table_text, input_tokens, output_tokens). The table text

 1872:       - the LLM call failed,
 1873:       - the response had no valid table structure,
 1874:       - every data row cited out-of-range [N] numbers.
 1875: 
 1876:     No fabrication surface: input prose is already strict_verified;
 1877:     out-of-range citations are dropped; no deterministic fallback
 1878:     emits claims that are not in the prose.
 1879:     """
 1880:     from src.polaris_graph.llm.openrouter_client import OpenRouterClient
 1881: 
 1882:     if not verified_prose or not verified_prose.strip():
 1883:         return "", 0, 0
 1884:     if not bibliography:
 1885:         return "", 0, 0
 1886: 
 1887:     valid_nums = {
 1888:         int(e.get("num"))
 1889:         for e in bibliography
 1890:         if isinstance(e.get("num"), int)
 1891:     }
 1892:     if not valid_nums:
 1893:         return "", 0, 0
 1894: 
 1895:     prompt = (
 1896:         "Verified prose (use ONLY facts present here):\n\n"
 1897:         f"{verified_prose}\n\n"
 1898:         "Produce the Trial Summary table now. Cite using the [N] markers "
 1899:         "that appear above; do not invent numbers. If no clinical trials "
 1900:         "are named in the prose above, output only `NO_TRIALS_NAMED`."
 1901:     )
 1902: 
 1903:     client = OpenRouterClient(model=model)
 1904:     try:
 1905:         response = await client.generate(
 1906:             prompt=prompt,
 1907:             system=TRIAL_SUMMARY_TABLE_SYSTEM_PROMPT,
 1908:             max_tokens=max_tokens,
 1909:             temperature=temperature,
 1910:         )
 1911:         raw = (response.content or "").strip()

 1913:         out_tok = response.output_tokens
 1914:     except Exception as exc:
 1915:         logger.warning("[multi_section] trial-summary table call failed: %s", exc)
 1916:         raw, in_tok, out_tok = "", 0, 0
 1917:     finally:
 1918:         if hasattr(client, "close"):
 1919:             try:
 1920:                 await client.close()
 1921:             except Exception:
 1922:                 pass
 1923: 
 1924:     table = _extract_trial_summary_table(raw, valid_nums)
 1925:     if not table:
 1926:         logger.info(
 1927:             "[multi_section] trial-summary table suppressed "
 1928:             "(raw_len=%d, no_valid_rows=True)", len(raw),
 1929:         )
 1930:     else:
 1931:         n_rows = table.count("\n") - 1  # header + sep + data; rows = total - 1
 1932:         logger.info(
 1933:             "[multi_section] trial-summary table: %d data rows", max(0, n_rows),

 3482:     async def _m63_llm_call(prompt: str) -> tuple[str, int, int]:

 3497:         headroom without inviting runaway verbosity.
 3498:         """

 3508:                     "code fences, or any text outside the JSON "
 3509:                     "object."
 3510:                 ),
 3511:                 max_tokens=max(section_max_tokens, 6000),

  437: @dataclass
  438: class UsageTracker:
  439:     """Track token usage and cost across the session."""
  440: 
  441:     total_input_tokens: int = 0
  442:     total_output_tokens: int = 0
  443:     total_reasoning_tokens: int = 0
  444:     total_calls: int = 0
  445:     total_errors: int = 0
  446:     budget_usd: float = OPENROUTER_BUDGET_USD
  447:     session_id: str = ""  # FIX-F2: Distinguish runs in persistent cost ledger
  448:     _call_log: list = field(default_factory=list)
  449: 
  450:     # FIX-C2: Track API-reported cost for accurate billing
  451:     total_api_reported_cost: float = 0.0
  452: 
  453:     @property
  454:     def total_cost_usd(self) -> float:
  455:         # Prefer API-reported cost if available (accurate per-provider pricing)
  456:         if self.total_api_reported_cost > 0:
  457:             return self.total_api_reported_cost
  458:         input_cost = (self.total_input_tokens / 1_000_000) * INPUT_COST_PER_M
  459:         output_cost = (self.total_output_tokens / 1_000_000) * OUTPUT_COST_PER_M
  460:         return input_cost + output_cost
  461: 
  462:     @property
  463:     def budget_remaining_usd(self) -> float:
  464:         return self.budget_usd - self.total_cost_usd
  465: 
  466:     @property
  467:     def budget_exhausted(self) -> bool:
  468:         return self.total_cost_usd >= self.budget_usd
  469: 
  470:     def record(
  471:         self,
  472:         call_type: str,
  473:         input_tokens: int,
  474:         output_tokens: int,
  475:         reasoning_tokens: int = 0,
  476:         duration_ms: float = 0,
  477:         api_cost: float = 0.0,
  478:         prompt_component_tokens: dict | None = None,
  479:     ):
  480:         self.total_input_tokens += input_tokens
  481:         self.total_output_tokens += output_tokens
  482:         self.total_reasoning_tokens += reasoning_tokens
  483:         self.total_calls += 1
  484:         # FIX-C2: Accumulate API-reported cost for accurate billing
  485:         if api_cost > 0:
  486:             self.total_api_reported_cost += api_cost
  487:         call_cost = api_cost if api_cost > 0 else round(
  488:             (input_tokens / 1_000_000) * INPUT_COST_PER_M
  489:             + (output_tokens / 1_000_000) * OUTPUT_COST_PER_M,
  490:             6,
  491:         )
  492:         entry = {
  493:             "type": call_type,
  494:             "input_tokens": input_tokens,
  495:             "output_tokens": output_tokens,
  496:             "reasoning_tokens": reasoning_tokens,
  497:             "duration_ms": duration_ms,
  498:             "cost_usd": round(call_cost, 6),
  499:             "cumulative_cost_usd": round(self.total_cost_usd, 4),
  500:         }
  501:         # TIER-3 Stage 6: Optional prompt component breakdown
  502:         if prompt_component_tokens:
  503:             entry["prompt_components"] = prompt_component_tokens
  504:         self._call_log.append(entry)
  505: 
  506:         # FIX-305: Persist to JSONL cost ledger
  507:         self._append_ledger({
  508:             "timestamp": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
  509:             "session_id": self.session_id,  # FIX-F2: Tag entries with run ID
  510:             "call_type": call_type,
  511:             "input_tokens": input_tokens,
  512:             "output_tokens": output_tokens,
  513:             "reasoning_tokens": reasoning_tokens,
  514:             "duration_ms": round(duration_ms, 1),
  515:             "cost_usd": round(call_cost, 6),
  516:             "cumulative_cost_usd": round(self.total_cost_usd, 4),
  517:         })
  518: 
  519:     def _append_ledger(self, entry: dict):
  520:         """Append a cost entry to the persistent JSONL ledger."""
  521:         try:
  522:             _COST_LEDGER_PATH.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

  304: async def generate_analyst_synthesis(
  305:     *,
  306:     verified_prose: str,
  307:     bibliography: list[dict[str, Any]],
  308:     evidence_rows: list[dict[str, Any]],
  309:     research_question: str,
  310:     model: str = "deepseek/deepseek-v3.2-exp",
  311:     max_tokens: int = 4000,
  312:     temperature: float = 0.3,
  313: ) -> tuple[str, int, int]:
  314:     """Generate the Analyst Synthesis section.
  315: 
  316:     Per Codex iter-1 brief verdict: DeepSeek V3.2-Exp is the writer
  317:     (consistent with verified prose voice; Gemma stays in the
  318:     judge/evaluator role).
  319: 
  320:     Returns (text, input_tokens, output_tokens). Returns ("", 0, 0)
  321:     on failure — caller MUST treat empty text as "omit synthesis
  322:     section entirely" (no empty disclosure block per Codex iter-1).
  323:     """
  324:     from src.polaris_graph.llm.openrouter_client import OpenRouterClient
  325: 
  326:     biblio_block = _format_bibliography_for_prompt(bibliography)
  327:     evidence_block = _format_evidence_pool_for_prompt(evidence_rows)
  328: 
  329:     prompt = (
  330:         f"Research question: {research_question}\n\n"
  331:         f"=== VERIFIED FINDINGS (above the synthesis section) ===\n\n"
  332:         f"{verified_prose}\n\n"
  333:         f"=== BIBLIOGRAPHY (cite by [N] only) ===\n\n"
  334:         f"{biblio_block}\n\n"
  335:         f"=== EVIDENCE POOL (for synthesis context) ===\n\n"
  336:         f"{evidence_block}\n\n"
  337:         f"=== TASK ===\n\n"
  338:         f"Write the Analyst Synthesis section now, following the rules. "
  339:         f"Hedge interpretive claims; cite by [N] only; no [#ev:...] tokens; "
  340:         f"4-6 sub-sections with ### subheadings; 1500-3000 words total."
  341:     )
  342: 
  343:     client = OpenRouterClient(model=model)
  344:     try:
  345:         response = await client.generate(
  346:             prompt=prompt,
  347:             system=ANALYST_SYNTHESIS_SYSTEM_PROMPT,
  348:             max_tokens=max_tokens,
  349:             temperature=temperature,
  350:         )
  351:         text = (response.content or "").strip()
  352:         in_tok = response.input_tokens
  353:         out_tok = response.output_tokens
  354:     except Exception as exc:
  355:         logger.warning("[analyst_synthesis] generation failed: %s", exc)
  356:         return "", 0, 0
  357:     finally:
  358:         try:
  359:             await client.close()
  360:         except Exception:
  361:             pass
  362: 
  363:     if not text:
  364:         logger.warning("[analyst_synthesis] empty response — section omitted")
  365:         return "", in_tok, out_tok
  366: 
  367:     # Codex iter-1 P0 guardrail: scrub [#ev:...] tokens from synthesis.
  368:     cleaned = _scrub_ev_tokens(text)
  369:     # I-bug-108 P0: scrub [N] markers exceeding bibliography size
  370:     # to prevent rule_pt12_invalid_citation_marker from aborting the
  371:     # report. Synthesis LLM occasionally hallucinates indices; scrub
  372:     # them runtime so production runs don't abort.
  373:     cleaned, _ = _scrub_invalid_n_markers(cleaned, biblio_size=len(bibliography))
  374:     return cleaned, in_tok, out_tok

  190: def _parse_iso(value: Any) -> datetime | None:
  191:     if not value:
  192:         return None
  193:     if isinstance(value, datetime):
  194:         return value
  195:     try:
  196:         return datetime.fromisoformat(str(value).replace("Z", "+00:00"))

    1: """Manifest builder — collects all bundle content + computes SHA256s.
    2: 
    3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_004/architecture_proposal.md` §"manifest_builder".
    4: 
    5: Given a ScopeDecision + EvidencePool + VerifiedReport (the research chain
    6: output), serializes each to canonical JSON, snapshots cited source
    7: texts, and assembles a BundleManifest with SHA256 anchors over every
    8: content file.
    9: 
   10: The manifest itself is YAML-serialized (canonical sort keys); GPG signs
   11: that YAML. External verifiers re-serialize the manifest and re-verify
   12: the signature.
   13: """

   16:

   18: import json

   47: # these; do not rename without bumping bundle_version.

   56: def _sha256_bytes(data: bytes) -> str:
   57:     return hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest()
   58: 
   59: 
   60: def _serialize_json_canonical(model: Any) -> bytes:
   61:     """Pydantic model -> deterministic UTF-8 JSON bytes.
   62: 
   63:     sort_keys + no extra whitespace beyond standard separators ensures
   64:     re-serialization on the verifier side produces identical bytes →
   65:     SHA256 stable across implementations.
   66:     """
   67:     if hasattr(model, "model_dump"):
   68:         payload = model.model_dump(mode="json")
   69:     else:
   70:         payload = model
   71:     return json.dumps(
   72:         payload,
   73:         sort_keys=True,
   74:         ensure_ascii=False,
   75:         separators=(",", ":"),
   76:     ).encode("utf-8")
   77: 
   78: 
   79: def _assert_cited_spans_reachable(report: VerifiedReport, snapshots: dict) -> None:
   80:     """Raise ValueError if any cited span exceeds its snapshot's reachable_chars.
   81: 
   82:     Validates the UNION of tokens parsed from `sentence.sentence_text` and
   83:     `sentence.provenance_tokens`, deduped by `token.raw`. Missing source_id =>
   84:     unreachable. Span end > reachable_chars => unreachable.
   85:     """
   86:     seen: set[str] = set()
   87:     for section in report.sections:
   88:         if section.section_status == "dropped":
   89:             continue
   90:         for sentence in section.verified_sentences:
   91:             if not sentence.verifier_pass:
   92:                 continue
   93:             tokens = list(extract_tokens(sentence.sentence_text))
   94:             for raw in sentence.provenance_tokens:
   95:                 tokens.extend(extract_tokens(raw))
   96:             for tok in tokens:
   97:                 if tok.raw in seen:
   98:                     continue
   99:                 seen.add(tok.raw)
  100:                 entry = snapshots.get(tok.source_id)
  101:                 if entry is None:
  102:                     raise ValueError(
  103:                         f"cited span unreachable after snapshot: source "
  104:                         f"{tok.source_id!r} not in snapshots (token={tok.raw!r})"
  105:                     )
  106:                 if not (0 <= tok.span_start < tok.span_end <= entry.reachable_chars):
  107:                     raise ValueError(
  108:                         f"cited span unreachable after snapshot: source "
  109:                         f"{tok.source_id!r} token={tok.raw!r} span="
  110:                         f"{tok.span_start}-{tok.span_end} reachable={entry.reachable_chars}"
  111:                     )
  112: 
  113: 
  114: def _safe_source_filename(source_id: str) -> str:
  115:     """Build a tar-safe filename from a source_id.
  116: 
  117:     source_id is opaque (uuid by default, but could be 'src-1' etc). We
  118:     sanitize aggressively: only [a-zA-Z0-9_-]. Anything else becomes _.
  119:     Length-capped at 100 chars to avoid pathological inputs.
  120:     """
  121:     safe = "".join(
  122:         c if c.isalnum() or c in "-_" else "_" for c in source_id
  123:     )[:100]
  124:     return f"{SOURCES_DIR}/{safe}.txt"
  125: 
  126: 
  127: def build_manifest_and_files(
  128:     decision: ScopeDecision,
  129:     pool: EvidencePool,
  130:     report: VerifiedReport,
  131: ) -> tuple[BundleManifest, dict[str, bytes]]:
  132:     """Build the bundle manifest + content-file dict.
  133: 
  134:     Returns:
  135:         (manifest, files) where files is {path: content_bytes}. The
  136:         caller (bundle_builder) packs files into a tarball and writes
  137:         the manifest.yaml + manifest.yaml.asc alongside.
  138: 
  139:     Raises:
  140:         ValueError if report.pipeline_verdict != 'success'.
  141:     """
  142:     if report.pipeline_verdict != "success":
  143:         raise ValueError(
  144:             f"cannot build audit bundle for verdict "
  145:             f"{report.pipeline_verdict!r}; report must be successful"
  146:         )
  147: 
  148:     files_bytes: dict[str, bytes] = {}
  149: 
  150:     # 1. Slice 001 ScopeDecision
  151:     sd_bytes = _serialize_json_canonical(decision)
  152:     files_bytes[FILE_SCOPE_DECISION] = sd_bytes
  153: 
  154:     # 2. Slice 002 EvidencePool
  155:     ep_bytes = _serialize_json_canonical(pool)
  156:     files_bytes[FILE_EVIDENCE_POOL] = ep_bytes
  157: 
  158:     # 3. Slice 003 VerifiedReport
  159:     vr_bytes = _serialize_json_canonical(report)
  160:     files_bytes[FILE_VERIFIED_REPORT] = vr_bytes
  161: 
  162:     # 4. Sovereignty: refuse to ship verbatim spans for non-cleared sources
  163:     assert_all_pool_sources_legal_cleared(pool)
  164: 
  165:     # 4b. Per-source snapshots + cited-span reachability guard
  166:     snapshot_entries = snapshot_sources_with_reachable(report, pool)
  167:     _assert_cited_spans_reachable(report, snapshot_entries)
  168:     for source_id, entry in snapshot_entries.items():
  169:         files_bytes[_safe_source_filename(source_id)] = entry.text.encode("utf-8")
  170:     snapshots = {sid: e.text for sid, e in snapshot_entries.items()}
  171: 
  172:     # 4b. REVIEWER_README ships verbatim in every bundle as metadata content_type.
  173:     readme_path = Path(__file__).parent / "REVIEWER_README.md"
  174:     files_bytes[FILE_REVIEWER_README] = readme_path.read_bytes()
  175: 
  176:     # 5. Bundle metadata (versions + creation timestamp)
  177:     metadata = {
  178:         "bundle_version": BUNDLE_VERSION,
  179:         "polaris_version": POLARIS_VERSION,
  180:         "created_at_utc": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat().replace(
  181:             "+00:00", "Z"
  182:         ),
  183:         "generator_model": report.generator_model,
  184:         "decision_id": decision.decision_id,
  185:         "pool_id": report.pool_id,
  186:         "report_id": report.report_id,
  187:         "source_snapshot_count": len(snapshots),
  188:     }
  189:     files_bytes[FILE_METADATA] = json.dumps(
  190:         metadata,
  191:         sort_keys=True,
  192:         ensure_ascii=False,
  193:         separators=(",", ":"),
  194:     ).encode("utf-8")
  195: 
  196:     # Build FileEntry list with content_type tags
  197:     file_entries: list[FileEntry] = []
  198:     content_type_by_path = {
  199:         FILE_SCOPE_DECISION: "scope_decision",
  200:         FILE_EVIDENCE_POOL: "evidence_pool",
  201:         FILE_VERIFIED_REPORT: "verified_report",
  202:         FILE_METADATA: "metadata",
  203:     }
  204:     for path, content in files_bytes.items():
  205:         ct = content_type_by_path.get(
  206:             path,
  207:             "source_snapshot" if path.startswith(SOURCES_DIR + "/") else "metadata",
  208:         )
  209:         file_entries.append(
  210:             FileEntry(
  211:                 path=path,
  212:                 sha256=_sha256_bytes(content),
  213:                 size_bytes=len(content),
  214:                 content_type=ct,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
  215:             )
  216:         )
  217: 
  218:     # Sort entries deterministically for stable manifest output
  219:     file_entries.sort(key=lambda f: f.path)
  220: 
  221:     manifest = BundleManifest(
  222:         decision_id=decision.decision_id,
  223:         pool_id=report.pool_id,
  224:         report_id=report.report_id,
  225:         generator_model=report.generator_model,
  226:         polaris_version=POLARIS_VERSION,
  227:         files=file_entries,
  228:     )
  229:     return manifest, files_bytes
  230: 
  231: 
  232: def serialize_manifest_yaml(manifest: BundleManifest) -> bytes:
  233:     """Produce canonical YAML bytes for GPG signing.
  234: 
  235:     PyYAML default_flow_style=False + sort_keys=True keeps it stable
  236:     across re-serializations.
  237:     """
  238:     payload = manifest.model_dump(mode="json")
  239:     return yaml.safe_dump(
  240:         payload,
  241:         default_flow_style=False,
  242:         sort_keys=True,
  243:         allow_unicode=True,
  244:     ).encode("utf-8")

    1: """Bundle manifest schema for slice 004 audit-bundle export.
    2: 
    3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_004/architecture_proposal.md`.
    4: 
    5: Pure-types module. The BundleManifest is the audit anchor: an external
    6: verifier extracts the .tar.gz, computes SHA256 of every content file,
    7: checks against `files[*].sha256`, then verifies the GPG signature on the
    8: manifest itself. If the manifest verifies and content hashes match, the
    9: bundle is intact.
   10: """
   11:

   13: 
   14: import uuid
   15: from datetime import datetime, timezone
   16: from typing import Literal
   17: 
   18: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, field_validator
   19: 
   20:

   22: # Type literals
   23: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   24: 
   25: ContentType = Literal[
   26:     "scope_decision",      # slice 001 ScopeDecision JSON
   27:     "evidence_pool",       # slice 002 EvidencePool JSON
   28:     "verified_report",     # slice 003 VerifiedReport JSON
   29:     "source_snapshot",     # full_text of one cited source
   30:     "metadata",            # bundle-level metadata (versions, etc.)

   36: 
   37: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   38: # FileEntry
   39: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   40: 
   41: class FileEntry(BaseModel):
   42:     """One file in the bundle, with hash anchor."""
   43: 
   44:     path: str = Field(
   45:         min_length=1,
   46:         max_length=500,
   47:         description=(
   48:             "Relative path inside the .tar.gz. e.g. 'manifest.yaml',"
   49:             " 'sources/abc-123.txt', 'verified_report.json'."
   50:         ),
   51:     )
   52:     sha256: str = Field(
   53:         min_length=64,
   54:         max_length=64,
   55:         description="Lowercase hex SHA256 digest of file contents.",
   56:     )
   57:     size_bytes: int = Field(ge=0)
   58:     content_type: ContentType
   59: 
   60:     @field_validator("sha256")
   61:     @classmethod
   62:     def _sha256_lowercase_hex(cls, v: str) -> str:
   63:         v = v.strip().lower()
   64:         if len(v) != 64:
   65:             raise ValueError("sha256 must be exactly 64 hex chars")
   66:         if any(c not in "0123456789abcdef" for c in v):
   67:             raise ValueError("sha256 must be lowercase hex")
   68:         return v
   69: 
   70:     @field_validator("path")
   71:     @classmethod
   72:     def _path_no_traversal(cls, v: str) -> str:
   73:         v = v.strip()
   74:         if v.startswith("/") or ".." in v.split("/"):
   75:             raise ValueError(
   76:                 "path must be relative and must not contain '..' segments"
   77:             )
   78:         return v
   79: 
   80: 
   81: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   82: # BundleManifest
   83: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   84: 
   85: class BundleManifest(BaseModel):
   86:     """Top-level bundle manifest — what GPG signs.
   87: 
   88:     The signature in `manifest.yaml.asc` is over the YAML-serialized form
   89:     of this manifest. External verifiers re-serialize and re-verify.
   90:     """
   91: 
   92:     bundle_id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
   93:     bundle_version: Literal["1.0"] = BUNDLE_VERSION
   94: 
   95:     # Foreign keys back through the research pipeline
   96:     decision_id: str = Field(min_length=1, description="slice 001 ScopeDecision id")
   97:     pool_id: str = Field(min_length=1, description="slice 002 EvidencePool id")
   98:     report_id: str = Field(min_length=1, description="slice 003 VerifiedReport id")
   99: 
  100:     # Provenance metadata
  101:     generator_model: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=200)
  102:     polaris_version: str = Field(min_length=1, max_length=50)
  103: 
  104:     # Content files (excluding manifest.yaml + manifest.yaml.asc themselves)
  105:     files: list[FileEntry] = Field(default_factory=list, max_length=10000)
  106: 
  107:     bundle_created_at_utc: datetime = Field(
  108:         default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(timezone.utc)
  109:     )
  110: 
  111:     @field_validator("files")
  112:     @classmethod
  113:     def _files_unique_paths(cls, v: list[FileEntry]) -> list[FileEntry]:
  114:         paths = [f.path for f in v]
  115:         if len(set(paths)) != len(paths):
  116:             duplicates = sorted({p for p in paths if paths.count(p) > 1})
  117:             raise ValueError(
  118:                 f"files must have unique paths; duplicates: {duplicates}"
  119:             )
  120:         return v
  121: 
  122:     def file_by_content_type(
  123:         self, content_type: ContentType
  124:     ) -> list[FileEntry]:
  125:         """Filter files to a specific content_type. Used by verifiers."""
  126:         return [f for f in self.files if f.content_type == content_type]
  127: 
  128:     def total_bytes(self) -> int:
  129:         return sum(f.size_bytes for f in self.files)

  881:     async def _accumulate_sse(
  882:         self, response: httpx.Response,
  883:     ) -> tuple[str, str, dict]:
  884:         """Accumulate SSE chunks from a streaming response.
  885: 
  886:         Returns (content, reasoning_content, usage_data).
  887: 
  888:         Handles OpenRouter SSE format:
  889:         - ``data: {JSON}`` — delta chunks with content/reasoning_content
  890:         - ``data: [DONE]`` — stream terminator
  891:         - ``: OPENROUTER PROCESSING`` — keep-alive comments (ignored)
  892:         - Empty lines between events (ignored)
  893: 
  894:         Phase 3: Added chunk metrics (count, bytes), mid-stream error
  895:         detection, and [DONE] terminator verification.
  896:         """
  897:         content_parts: list[str] = []
  898:         reasoning_parts: list[str] = []
  899:         usage_data: dict = {}
  900: 
  901:         # Phase 3: SSE chunk metrics
  902:         chunk_count = 0
  903:         content_bytes = 0
  904:         reasoning_bytes = 0
  905:         done_received = False
  906: 
  907:         async for line in response.aiter_lines():
  908:             # Skip empty lines and SSE comments (keep-alive)
  909:             if not line or line.startswith(":"):
  910:                 continue
  911:             # SSE data lines start with "data: "
  912:             if not line.startswith("data: "):
  913:                 continue
  914:             payload = line[6:]  # Strip "data: " prefix
  915:             if payload.strip() == "[DONE]":
  916:                 done_received = True
  917:                 break
  918:             try:
  919:                 chunk = json.loads(payload)
  920:             except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError):
  921:                 logger.debug("[polaris graph] SSE: skipping unparseable chunk")
  922:                 continue
  923: 
  924:             chunk_count += 1
  925: 
  926:             # Phase 3: Mid-stream error detection (SOTA research finding)
  927:             # FIX-QWEN-1: Also detect top-level errors with empty choices
  928:             # (Alibaba provider returns 502 as {"choices":[], "error":{...}})
  929:             chunk_error = chunk.get("error")
  930:             choices = chunk.get("choices", [])
  931:             if chunk_error and not choices:
  932:                 error_msg = chunk_error.get("message", str(chunk_error))[:200]
  933:                 error_code = chunk_error.get("code", "?")
  934:                 logger.warning(
  935:                     "[polaris graph] FIX-QWEN-1: Provider error in SSE chunk %d "
  936:                     "(code=%s): %s",
  937:                     chunk_count, error_code, error_msg,
  938:                 )
  939:                 raise RuntimeError(f"SSE provider error (code={error_code}): {error_msg}")
  940:             if choices:
  941:                 finish_reason = choices[0].get("finish_reason")
  942:                 if finish_reason == "error":
  943:                     error_info = chunk.get("error", {})
  944:                     error_msg = error_info.get("message", "unknown mid-stream error")
  945:                     logger.error(
  946:                         "[polaris graph] SSE mid-stream error at chunk %d: %s",
  947:                         chunk_count,
  948:                         error_msg[:200],
  949:                     )
  950:                     raise RuntimeError(f"SSE mid-stream error: {error_msg[:200]}")
  951: 
  952:                 delta = choices[0].get("delta", {})
  953:                 if delta.get("content"):
  954:                     text = delta["content"]
  955:                     content_parts.append(text)
  956:                     content_bytes += len(text.encode("utf-8"))
  957:                 # Check both reasoning_content and reasoning (provider-dependent)
  958:                 rc = delta.get("reasoning_content") or delta.get("reasoning")
  959:                 if rc:
  960:                     reasoning_parts.append(rc)
  961:                     reasoning_bytes += len(rc.encode("utf-8"))
  962: 
  963:             # Usage data (typically in final chunk with finish_reason)
  964:             if "usage" in chunk and chunk["usage"]:
  965:                 usage_data = chunk["usage"]
  966: 
  967:         # Phase 3: Log SSE metrics
  968:         content_text = "".join(content_parts)
  969:         reasoning_text = "".join(reasoning_parts)
  970: 
  971:         if chunk_count > 0:
  972:             logger.info(
  973:                 "[polaris graph] SSE metrics: %d chunks, "
  974:                 "content=%d bytes (%d chars), reasoning=%d bytes (%d chars), "
  975:                 "done=%s, has_usage=%s",
  976:                 chunk_count,
  977:                 content_bytes,
  978:                 len(content_text),
  979:                 reasoning_bytes,
  980:                 len(reasoning_text),
  981:                 done_received,
  982:                 bool(usage_data),
  983:             )
  984: 
  985:         if not done_received and chunk_count > 0:
  986:             logger.warning(
  987:                 "[polaris graph] SSE stream ended without [DONE] terminator "
  988:                 "after %d chunks — possible connection drop",
  989:                 chunk_count,
  990:             )
  991: 
  992:         return content_text, reasoning_text, usage_data
  993: 
  994:     async def _read_stream(
  995:         self, body: dict, timeout: float,
  996:     ) -> tuple[str, str, dict]:
  997:         """Execute streaming POST and accumulate SSE response.
  998: 
  999:         Opens an httpx streaming connection, reads SSE events, and returns
 1000:         the accumulated (content, reasoning_content, usage) tuple.
 1001: 
 1002:         Handles two response formats:
 1003:         - ``text/event-stream``: True SSE — accumulate delta chunks
 1004:         - ``application/json``: Non-SSE fallback — provider returned a
 1005:           standard JSON response despite ``stream: true`` (happens when
 1006:           the provider doesn't support streaming for reasoning models)
 1007: 
 1008:         The httpx Timeout uses the caller's timeout for read operations
 1009:         and a generous 30s for connection establishment.
 1010:         """
 1011:         async with self._client.stream(
 1012:             "POST",
 1013:             "/chat/completions",
 1014:             json=body,
 1015:             timeout=httpx.Timeout(timeout, connect=30.0),
 1016:         ) as response:
 1017:             response.raise_for_status()
 1018: 
 1019:             content_type = response.headers.get("content-type", "")
 1020: 
 1021:             if "text/event-stream" in content_type:
 1022:                 # True SSE stream — accumulate delta chunks
 1023:                 logger.debug(
 1024:                     "[polaris graph] SSE path: Content-Type=%s",
 1025:                     content_type,
 1026:                 )
 1027:                 content, reasoning, usage = await self._accumulate_sse(response)
 1028: 
 1029:                 # Defense: if SSE produced nothing, the stream may have
 1030:                 # been malformed. Log for diagnostics.
 1031:                 if not content and not reasoning and not usage:
 1032:                     logger.warning(
 1033:                         "[polaris graph] SSE stream produced no content, "
 1034:                         "reasoning, or usage. Content-Type: %s",
 1035:                         content_type,
 1036:                     )
 1037: 
 1038:                 return content, reasoning, usage
 1039: 
 1040:             # Non-SSE response — provider returned standard JSON
 1041:             # despite stream:true. Read full body and parse.
 1042:             logger.info(
 1043:                 "[polaris graph] Non-SSE path: Content-Type=%s",
 1044:                 content_type,
 1045:             )
 1046:             raw_body = await response.aread()
 1047:             try:
 1048:                 data = json.loads(raw_body)
 1049:             except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError) as exc:
 1050:                 logger.error(
 1051:                     "[polaris graph] Non-SSE response body is not JSON "
 1052:                     "(%d bytes, Content-Type: %s): %s",
 1053:                     len(raw_body),
 1054:                     content_type,
 1055:                     str(exc)[:200],
 1056:                 )
 1057:                 return "", "", {}
 1058: 
 1059:             choices = data.get("choices", [])
 1060:             if not choices:
 1061:                 return "", "", data.get("usage", {})
 1062: 
 1063:             message = choices[0].get("message", {})
 1064:             logger.info(
 1065:                 "[polaris graph] Non-SSE response detected "
 1066:                 "(Content-Type: %s). Parsing as standard JSON. "
 1067:                 "content=%d chars, reasoning=%d chars",
 1068:                 content_type,
 1069:                 len(message.get("content", "") or ""),
 1070:                 len(message.get("reasoning_content", "") or ""),
 1071:             )
 1072: 
 1073:             return (
 1074:                 message.get("content", "") or "",
 1075:                 message.get("reasoning_content", "")
 1076:                 or message.get("reasoning", "")
 1077:                 or "",
 1078:                 data.get("usage", {}),
 1079:             )

 succeeded in 2613ms:
    1: """
    2: Structured pipeline tracer for polaris graph.
    3: 
    4: Emits JSONL events to logs/pg_trace_{vector_id}.jsonl alongside
    5: regular Python logging. Every node, LLM call, fetch, and quality
    6: decision gets a machine-parseable trace event.
    7: 
    8: OBS-1: Standalone tracing module with zero external dependencies.
    9: Uses stdlib only: json, time, contextvars, dataclasses, pathlib.
   10: """
   11: 
   12: import json
   13: import logging
   14: import os
   15: import time
   16: import uuid
   17: from contextvars import ContextVar
   18: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
   19: from datetime import datetime, timezone
   20: from pathlib import Path
   21: from typing import Any, Optional
   22: 
   23: logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
   24: 
   25: PG_TRACING_ENABLED = os.getenv("PG_TRACING_ENABLED", "1") == "1"
   26: 
   27: # Thread-safe vector_id propagation
   28: _current_vector_id: ContextVar[str] = ContextVar("pg_vector_id", default="unknown")
   29: _current_tracer: ContextVar[Optional["PipelineTracer"]] = ContextVar("pg_tracer", default=None)
   30: 
   31: 
   32: @dataclass
   33: class TraceEvent:
   34:     """A single structured trace event."""
   35: 
   36:     timestamp: str
   37:     vector_id: str
   38:     node: str           # "plan", "search", "analyze", "verify", "evaluate", "synthesize"
   39:     event_type: str     # "node_start", "node_end", "fetch", "llm_call", "quality_gate", etc.
   40:     data: dict = field(default_factory=dict)
   41:     duration_ms: float = 0.0
   42: 
   43: 
   44: class PipelineTracer:
   45:     """Structured JSONL tracer for pipeline observability.
   46: 
   47:     Creates a JSONL file at logs/pg_trace_{vector_id}.jsonl and writes
   48:     one event per line. Also keeps events in memory for summary.
   49: 
   50:     Usage::
   51: 
   52:         tracer = PipelineTracer("V001")
   53:         tracer.node_start("plan", iteration=1)
   54:         # ... do work ...
   55:         tracer.node_end("plan", query_count=50)
   56:         print(tracer.summary())
   57:     """
   58: 
   59:     def __init__(self, vector_id: str, output_dir: str = "logs"):
   60:         self.vector_id = vector_id
   61:         # W3.3: session_id disambiguates events when multiple runs append to
   62:         # the same pg_trace_{vector_id}.jsonl. Readers can filter by sid to
   63:         # isolate a single pipeline execution.
   64:         self.session_id = uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]
   65:         self._events: list[TraceEvent] = []
   66:         self._node_timers: dict[str, float] = {}
   67:         self._path = Path(output_dir) / f"pg_trace_{vector_id}.jsonl"
   68:         self._path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   69:         _current_vector_id.set(vector_id)
   70:         _current_tracer.set(self)
   71:         # Mark the start of this session so a new file section is parseable.
   72:         self._emit(
   73:             event_type="session_start",
   74:             node="pipeline",
   75:             data={"session_id": self.session_id},
   76:         )
   77: 
   78:     def node_start(self, node: str, **data: Any) -> None:
   79:         """Record node entry."""
   80:         self._node_timers[node] = time.monotonic()
   81:         self._emit("node_start", node, data)
   82: 
   83:     def node_end(self, node: str, **data: Any) -> None:
   84:         """Record node exit with wall-clock duration."""
   85:         start = self._node_timers.pop(node, time.monotonic())
   86:         duration_ms = (time.monotonic() - start) * 1000
   87:         self._emit("node_end", node, {**data, "duration_ms": round(duration_ms, 1)})
   88: 
   89:     def fetch(
   90:         self,
   91:         node: str,
   92:         url: str,
   93:         status: str,
   94:         content_len: int = 0,
   95:         duration_ms: float = 0,
   96:         **data: Any,
   97:     ) -> None:
   98:         """Record a URL fetch attempt."""
   99:         self._emit("fetch", node, {
  100:             "url": url[:200],
  101:             "status": status,
  102:             "content_len": content_len,
  103:             "duration_ms": round(duration_ms, 1),
  104:             **data,
  105:         })
  106: 
  107:     def llm_call(
  108:         self,
  109:         node: str,
  110:         call_type: str,
  111:         input_tokens: int = 0,
  112:         output_tokens: int = 0,
  113:         duration_ms: float = 0,
  114:         **data: Any,
  115:     ) -> None:
  116:         """Record an LLM API call."""
  117:         self._emit("llm_call", node, {
  118:             "call_type": call_type,
  119:             "input_tokens": input_tokens,
  120:             "output_tokens": output_tokens,
  121:             "duration_ms": round(duration_ms, 1),
  122:             **data,
  123:         })
  124: 
  125:     def evidence(self, node: str, action: str, count: int, **data: Any) -> None:
  126:         """Record evidence flow (extracted, filtered, deduped, accumulated)."""
  127:         self._emit("evidence", node, {"action": action, "count": count, **data})
  128: 
  129:     def quality_gate(self, node: str, gate: str, passed: bool, **data: Any) -> None:
  130:         """Record a quality gate check."""
  131:         self._emit("quality_gate", node, {"gate": gate, "passed": passed, **data})
  132: 
  133:     def query(self, node: str, action: str, queries: "list[str] | int", **data: Any) -> None:
  134:         """Record query generation/amplification."""
  135:         count = queries if isinstance(queries, int) else len(queries)
  136:         self._emit("query", node, {"action": action, "count": count, **data})
  137: 
  138:     def search_result(
  139:         self,
  140:         node: str,
  141:         engine: str,
  142:         query: str,
  143:         result_count: int,
  144:         **data: Any,
  145:     ) -> None:
  146:         """Record search results per query."""
  147:         self._emit("search_result", node, {
  148:             "engine": engine,
  149:             "query": query,
  150:             "result_count": result_count,
  151:             **data,
  152:         })
  153: 
  154:     def reasoning_capture(
  155:         self, node: str, call_type: str, reasoning_text: str,
  156:         prompt_excerpt: str = "", **data: Any,
  157:     ) -> None:
  158:         """Record LLM reasoning content from any call."""
  159:         self._emit("reasoning_capture", node, {
  160:             "call_type": call_type,
  161:             "reasoning_text": reasoning_text[:50000],
  162:             "chars": len(reasoning_text or ""),
  163:             "prompt_excerpt": prompt_excerpt[:500],
  164:             **data,
  165:         })
  166: 
  167:     def storm_transcript(
  168:         self, persona: str, round_num: int,
  169:         question: str, answer: str, sources: list[str],
  170:         key_findings: list[str], **data: Any,
  171:     ) -> None:
  172:         """Record a full STORM interview Q&A round."""
  173:         self._emit("storm_transcript", "storm_interviews", {
  174:             "persona": persona,
  175:             "round": round_num,
  176:             "question": question[:2000],
  177:             "answer": answer[:5000],
  178:             "sources": sources[:20],
  179:             "key_findings": key_findings[:10],
  180:             **data,
  181:         })
  182: 
  183:     def iteration_decision(
  184:         self, iteration: int, decision: str, rationale: dict,
  185:         **data: Any,
  186:     ) -> None:
  187:         """Record an iteration routing decision with full rationale."""
  188:         self._emit("iteration_decision", "evaluate", {
  189:             "iteration": iteration,
  190:             "decision": decision,
  191:             "rationale": rationale,
  192:             **data,
  193:         })
  194: 
  195:     def summary(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
  196:         """Return a summary of all trace events for state storage."""
  197:         node_durations: dict[str, float] = {}
  198:         event_counts: dict[str, int] = {}
  199:         for e in self._events:
  200:             event_counts[e.event_type] = event_counts.get(e.event_type, 0) + 1
  201:             if e.event_type == "node_end" and "duration_ms" in e.data:
  202:                 node_durations[e.node] = e.data["duration_ms"]
  203: 
  204:         return {
  205:             "total_events": len(self._events),
  206:             "nodes": list(set(e.node for e in self._events)),
  207:             "event_counts": event_counts,
  208:             "node_durations_ms": node_durations,
  209:             "trace_file": str(self._path),
  210:         }
  211: 
  212:     def log_event(
  213:         self, event_type: str, data: dict | None = None, node: str = "pipeline"
  214:     ) -> None:
  215:         """Generic event logging — public API for components like SmartArt."""
  216:         self._emit(event_type=event_type, node=node, data=data or {})
  217: 
  218:     def _emit(self, event_type: str, node: str, data: dict) -> None:
  219:         """Write a trace event to JSONL and memory."""
  220:         if not PG_TRACING_ENABLED:
  221:             return
  222:         event = TraceEvent(
  223:             timestamp=datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
  224:             vector_id=self.vector_id,
  225:             node=node,
  226:             event_type=event_type,
  227:             data=data,
  228:         )
  229:         self._events.append(event)
  230:         # Write to JSONL file

codex
The manifest and bundle path is mostly addressable by the brief’s acceptance criteria, but the client-level capture has one subtle contract problem: the trace needs both raw-channel data and post-normalization content provenance, and the current schema only has two content-source states. I’m checking whether that is already covered elsewhere before deciding severity.
